3.855l-5.833-3.387L15.119 7.2a.076.076 0 0 1 .071 0l4.83 2.791a4.494 4.494 0 0 1-.676 8.105v-5.678a.79.79 0 0 0-.407-.667zm2.01-3.023l-.141-.085-4.774-2.782a.776.776 0 0 0-.785 0L9.409 002-2v-3a1 1 0 10-2 0v3H5V7h3a1 1 0 000-2H5z"></path></svg></a></div></div></div></div><h2 id="event-composition" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Event composition<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#event-composition"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Zag encourages the use of spread props to ensure we automatically attach all the
event handlers and properties to elements.</p>
<p>Sometimes, you may want to attach your own event handlers to the elements. To do
that, import the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">mergeProps</code> utility provided by zag for your framework.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// 1. import mergeProps utility</span>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// 2. write your custom event handlers</span>

</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>a</span> <span class="token attr-name">href</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>https://twitter.com/zag_js<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span> <span class="token attr-name">target</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>_blank<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>triggerProps<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">

</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="id-composition" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Id composition<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#id-composition"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Zag depends heavily on pure DOM queries to identify elements. This means every
element part needs to have a unique id.</p>
<p>Each time you initiate the machine with the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">useMachine</code> hook, you&#x27;ll need to
ensure that you provide a unique id.</p>
<p>In most cases, you can rely on the framework providing a unique id for each
machine.</p>
<h3 id="react" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">React<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#react"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> accordion</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/accordion&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token punctuation">{</span> useMachine<span class="token punctuation">,</span> normalizeProps <span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/framework&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token punctuation">{</span> useId <span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;react&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token function"><span class="token maybe-class-name">Component</span></span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>accordion<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<p>See <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://react.dev/reference/react/useId" class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px">useId</a>.</p>
<h3 id="solid" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Solid<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#solid"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> accordion</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/accordion&quot;</span>

<h3 id="vue" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Vue<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#vue"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<pre class="prose language-html"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>script</span> <span class="token attr-name">setup</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">  <span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> accordion</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/accordion&quot;</span>

</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">  <span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token punctuation">{</span> useId <span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;vue&quot;</span>

<h3 id="svelte" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Svelte<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#svelte"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<pre class="prose language-html"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>script</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">  <span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> accordion</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/accordion&quot;</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">  <span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token punctuation">{</span> useMachine<span class="token punctuation">,</span> normalizeProps <span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/svelte&quot;</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">  <span class="token keyword">const</span> id <span class="token operator">=</span> $props<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">id</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">  <span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>accordion<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> id <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript">  <span class="token keyword">const</span> api <span class="token operator">=</span> machine<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">connect</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>service<span class="token punctuation">,</span> normalizeProps<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token script"><span class="token language-javascript"></span></span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>script</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">&lt;!-- ... --&gt;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>See <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/$props#$props.id()" class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px">$props.id</a>.</p>
<p>Internally, Zag maps the unique id provided to each component parts needed for
the widget to work.</p>
<p>In some cases, you might want to compose different machines together in a single
component. For example, you want to use the same trigger as a popover and
tooltip trigger at the same time.</p>
<p>To achieve this, you will need to pass custom <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code> to the machine&#x27;s context.
This will ensure that calling <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">document.getElementById(...)</code> within the tooltip
and/or popover will return the same element.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> tooltip</span> <span class="token keyword">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/tooltip&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> popover</span> <span class="token keyword">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/popover&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token function">Example</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token keyword">const</span> tooltipService <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tooltip<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    ids<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> trigger<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;id-1&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token keyword">const</span> popoverService <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>popover<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    ids<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> trigger<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;id-1&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// ...</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>In the example above, you will notice that the popover and tooltip trigger share
the same id. That&#x27;s how to compose machines together.</p>
<h3 id="important-customizing-ids-and-aria-attributes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Important: Customizing IDs and ARIA attributes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#important-customizing-ids-and-aria-attributes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<h4 id="always-use-the-ids-context-option" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Always use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code> context option<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#always-use-the-ids-context-option"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>When customizing element IDs, always use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code> option in the machine context.
Never manually set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code> attribute on elements using the prop functions.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// ❌ Wrong: Manually setting id on the element</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> api <span class="token operator">=</span> checkbox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">connect</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>service<span class="token punctuation">,</span> normalizeProps<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>label</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getLabelProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token attr-name">id</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>my-custom-id<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">Label</span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>label</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// ✓ Correct: Use the ids option in machine context</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>checkbox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  ids<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> label<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;my-custom-id&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> api <span class="token operator">=</span> checkbox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">connect</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>service<span class="token punctuation">,</span> normalizeProps<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>label</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getLabelProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">Label</span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>label</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span></div></pre>
<p><strong>Why?</strong> Zag needs to know about custom IDs to properly generate ARIA reference
attributes across all related elements. When you set IDs manually, the machine
can&#x27;t update the corresponding <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">aria-labelledby</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">aria-describedby</code>, and other
reference attributes.</p>
<h4 id="pitfall-custom-ids-with-missing-elements" class="textStyle_display.xs mt_6 mb_2">Pitfall: Custom IDs with missing elements<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#pitfall-custom-ids-with-missing-elements"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h4>
<p>When you configure custom IDs via the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code> option, Zag generates ARIA reference
attributes (like <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">aria-labelledby</code>) based on those IDs, regardless of whether
the elements exist in the DOM. This can break accessibility if you configure IDs
for elements you don&#x27;t render.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// ❌ Wrong: Configuring label ID but not rendering the label</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>checkbox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  ids<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> label<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;custom-label-id&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getControlProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token comment">/* Control has aria-labelledby=&quot;custom-label-id&quot; but label doesn&#x27;t exist */</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>input</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getHiddenInputProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">  </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// ✓ Correct: Only configure IDs for elements you render</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>checkbox<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  ids<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> control<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;custom-control-id&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// Don&#x27;t set label ID if you&#x27;re not rendering it</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getControlProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token attr-name">aria-label</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>Checkbox<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>input</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getHiddenInputProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">  </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// ✓ Better: Keep the label but hide it visually</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>label</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getLabelProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token attr-name">className</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span>visually-hidden<span class="token punctuation">&quot;</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">      Checkbox
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>label</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getControlProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">      </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>input</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getHiddenInputProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">  </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="custom-window-environment" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Custom window environment<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#custom-window-environment"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Internally, we use DOM query methods like <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">document.querySelectorAll</code> and
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">document.getElementById</code> to locate elements within the machine.</p>
<p>In custom environments like iframe, Shadow DOM, Electron, etc., the machine
might not work as expected because <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">document</code> may not be available.</p>
<p>To provide the correct reference to root node or document, you can pass
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getRootNode</code> function it to the machine&#x27;s context.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>In shadow DOM, the root node can be derived from calling
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">element.getRootNode()</code> method on any element.</p>
</blockquote>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> accordion</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/accordion&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token punctuation">{</span> useMachine<span class="token punctuation">,</span> normalizeProps <span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/react&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token maybe-class-name">Frame</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> useFrame <span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;react-frame-component&quot;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> data <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Watercraft&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">content</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Sample accordion content&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Automobiles&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">content</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Sample accordion content&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Aircraft&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">content</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;Sample accordion content&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">]</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token function"><span class="token maybe-class-name">Accordion</span></span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter"><span class="token punctuation">{</span> id <span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token keyword">const</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token dom variable">document</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useFrame</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>accordion<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    id<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token function-variable function">getRootNode</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token dom variable">document</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token keyword">const</span> api <span class="token operator">=</span> accordion<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">connect</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>service<span class="token punctuation">,</span> normalizeProps<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token keyword control-flow">return</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getRootProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">      </span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">map</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">item<span class="token punctuation">,</span> index</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token attr-name">key</span><span class="token script language-javascript"><span class="token script-punctuation punctuation">=</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>index<span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getItemProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">value</span><span class="token operator">:</span> item<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">title</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">          </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>h3</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">

composition\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eZag encourages the use of spread props to ensure we automatically attach all the\nevent handlers and properties to elements.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSometimes, you may want to attach your own event handlers to the elements. To do\nthat, import the \u003ccode\u003emergeProps\u003c/code\u003e utility provided by zag for your framework.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003e// 1. import mergeProps utility\nimport { useMachine, mergeProps } from \"@zag-js/react\"\nimport * as hoverCard from \"@zag-js/hover-card\"\n\nexport function Toggle() {\n  const service = useMachine(hoverCard.machine, {\n    id: \"1\",\n  })\n  const api = hoverCard.connect(service)\n\n  // 2. write your custom event handlers\n  const handleHover = () =\u003e {\n    // do something\n  }\n\n  // 3. merge the props\n  const triggerProps = mergeProps(api.getTriggerProps(), {\n    onPointerEnter: handleHover,\n  })\n\n  return (\n    // 4. spread the new props\n    \u0026#x3C;a href=\"https://twitter.com/zag_js\" target=\"_blank\" {...triggerProps}\u003e\n      {api.open ? \"Open\" : \"Close\"}\n    \u0026#x3C;/a\u003e\n  )\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eId composition\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eZag depends heavily on pure DOM queries to identify elements. This means every\nelement part needs to have a unique id.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach time you initiate the machine with the \u003ccode\u003euseMachine\u003c/code\u003e hook, you'll need to\nensure that you provide a unique id.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIn most cases, you can rely on the framework providing a unique id for each\nmachine.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eReact\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003eimport * as accordion from \"@zag-js/accordion\"\nimport { useMachine, normalizeProps } from \"@zag-js/framework\"\nimport { useId } from \"react\"\n\nfunction Component() {\n  const service = useMachine(accordion.machine, { id: useId() })\n  const api = machine.connect(service, normalizeProps)\n\n  // ...\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSee \u003ca href=\"https://react.dev/reference/react/useId\"\u003euseId\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSolid\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003eimport * as accordion from \"@zag-js/accordion\"\nimport { useMachine, normalizeProps } from \"@zag-js/solid\"\nimport { createUniqueId } from \"solid-js\"\n\nfunction Component() {\n  const service = useMachine(accordion.machine, { id: createUniqueId() })\n  const api = machine.connect(service, normalizeProps)\n\n  // ...\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSee\n\u003ca href=\"https://docs.solidjs.com/reference/component-apis/create-unique-id\"\u003ecreateUniqueId\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eVue\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-html\"\u003e\u0026#x3C;script setup\u003e\n  import * as accordion from \"@zag-js/accordion\"\n  import { useMachine, normalizeProps } from \"@zag-js/vue\"\n  import { useId } from \"vue\"\n\n  const service = useMachine(accordion.machine, { id: useId() })\n  const api = machine.connect(service, normalizeProps)\n\u0026#x3C;/script\u003e\n\n\u0026#x3C;template\u003e\n  \u0026#x3C;!-- ... --\u003e\n\u0026#x3C;/template\u003e\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSee \u003ca href=\"https://vuejs.org/api/composition-api-helpers#useid\"\u003euseId\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSvelte\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-html\"\u003e\u0026#x3C;script\u003e\n  import * as accordion from \"@zag-js/accordion\"\n  import { useMachine, normalizeProps } from \"@zag-js/svelte\"\n\n  const id = $props.id()\n  const service = useMachine(accordion.machine, { id })\n  const api = machine.connect(service, normalizeProps)\n\u0026#x3C;/script\u003e\n\n\u0026#x3C;!-- ... --\u003e\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSee \u003ca href=\"https://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/$props#$props.id()\"\u003e$props.id\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eInternally, Zag maps the unique id provided to each component parts needed for\nthe widget to work.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIn some cases, you might want to compose different machines together in a single\ncomponent. For example, you want to use the same trigger as a popover and\ntooltip trigger at the same time.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo achieve this, you will need to pass custom \u003ccode\u003eids\u003c/code\u003e to the machine's context.\nThis will ensure that calling \u003ccode\u003edocument.getElementById(...)\u003c/code\u003e within the tooltip\nand/or popover will return the same element.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\" metastring=\"{6,10}\"\u003eimport * as tooltip from \"@zag-js/tooltip\"\nimport * as popover from \"@zag-js/popover\"\n\nfunction Example() {\n  const tooltipService = useMachine(tooltip.machine, {\n    ids: { trigger: \"id-1\" },\n  })\n\n  const popoverService = useMachine(popover.machine, {\n    ids: { trigger: \"id-1\" },\n  })\n\n  // ...\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIn the example above, you will notice that the popover and tooltip trigger share\nthe same id. That's how to compose machines together.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eImportant: Customizing IDs and ARIA attributes\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eAlways use the \u003ccode\u003eids\u003c/code\u003e context option\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen customizing element IDs, always use the \u003ccode\u003eids\u003c/code\u003e option in the machine context.\nNever manually set the \u003ccode\u003eid\u003c/code\u003e attribute on elements using the prop functions.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003e// ❌ Wrong: Manually setting id on the element\nconst api = checkbox.connect(service, normalizeProps)\nreturn \u0026#x3C;label {...api.getLabelProps()} id=\"my-custom-id\"\u003eLabel\u0026#x3C;/label\u003e\n\n// ✓ Correct: Use the ids option in machine context\nconst service = useMachine(checkbox.machine, {\n  ids: { label: \"my-custom-id\" },\n})\nconst api = checkbox.connect(service, normalizeProps)\nreturn \u0026#x3C;label {...api.getLabelProps()}\u003eLabel\u0026#x3C;/label\u003e\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhy?\u003c/strong\u003e Zag needs to know about custom IDs to properly generate ARIA reference\nattributes across all related elements. When you set IDs manually, the machine\ncan't update the corresponding \u003ccode\u003earia-labelledby\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003earia-describedby\u003c/code\u003e, and other\nreference attributes.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003ePitfall: Custom IDs with missing elements\u003c/h4\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen you configure custom IDs via the \u003ccode\u003eids\u003c/code\u003e option, Zag generates ARIA reference\nattributes (like \u003ccode\u003earia-labelledby\u003c/code\u003e) based on those IDs, regardless of whether\nthe elements exist in the DOM. This can break accessibility if you configure IDs\nfor elements you don't render.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003e// ❌ Wrong: Configuring label ID but not rendering the label\nconst service = useMachine(checkbox.machine, {\n  ids: { label: \"custom-label-id\" },\n})\nreturn (\n  \u0026#x3C;div {...api.getControlProps()}\u003e\n    {/* Control has aria-labelledby=\"custom-label-id\" but label doesn't exist */}\n    \u0026#x3C;input {...api.getHiddenInputProps()} /\u003e\n  \u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n)\n\n// ✓ Correct: Only configure IDs for elements you render\nconst service = useMachine(checkbox.machine, {\n  ids: { control: \"custom-control-id\" },\n  // Don't set label ID if you're not rendering it\n})\nreturn (\n  \u0026#x3C;div {...api.getControlProps()} aria-label=\"Checkbox\"\u003e\n    \u0026#x3C;input {...api.getHiddenInputProps()} /\u003e\n  \u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n)\n\n// ✓ Better: Keep the label but hide it visually\nreturn (\n  \u0026#x3C;div\u003e\n    \u0026#x3C;label {...api.getLabelProps()} className=\"visually-hidden\"\u003e\n      Checkbox\n    \u0026#x3C;/label\u003e\n    \u0026#x3C;div {...api.getControlProps()}\u003e\n      \u0026#x3C;input {...api.getHiddenInputProps()} /\u003e\n    \u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n  \u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n)\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eCustom window environment\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eInternally, we use DOM query methods like \u003ccode\u003edocument.querySelectorAll\u003c/code\u003e and\n\u003ccode\u003edocument.getElementById\u003c/code\u003e to locate elements within the machine.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIn custom environments like iframe, Shadow DOM, Electron, etc., the machine\nmight not work as expected because \u003ccode\u003edocument\u003c/code\u003e may not be available.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo provide the correct reference to root node or document, you can pass\n\u003ccode\u003egetRootNode\u003c/code\u003e function it to the machine's context.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIn shadow DOM, the root node can be derived from calling\n\u003ccode\u003eelement.getRootNode()\u003c/code\u003e method on any element.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{12,16,42}\"\u003eimport * as accordion from \"@zag-js/accordion\"\nimport { useMachine, normalizeProps } from \"@zag-js/react\"\nimport Frame, { useFrame } from \"react-frame-component\"\n\nconst data = [\n  { title: \"Watercraft\", content: \"Sample accordion content\" },\n  { title: \"Automobiles\", content: \"Sample accordion content\" },\n  { title: \"Aircraft\", content: \"Sample accordion content\" },\n]\n\nfunction Accordion({ id }) {\n  const { document } = useFrame()\n\n encourages the use of spread props to ensure we automatically attach all the\nevent handlers and properties to elements.\n\nSometimes, you may want to attach your own event handlers to the elements. To do\nthat, import the `mergeProps` utility provided by zag for your framework.\n\n```jsx\n// 1. import mergeProps utility\nimport { useMachine, mergeProps } from \"@zag-js/react\"\nimport * as hoverCard from \"@zag-js/hover-card\"\n\nexport function Toggle() {\n  const service = useMachine(hoverCard.machine, {\n    id: \"1\",\n  })\n  const api = hoverCard.connect(service)\n\n  // 2. write your custom event handlers\n  const handleHover = () =\u003e {\n    // do something\n  }\n\n  // 3. merge the props\n  const triggerProps = mergeProps(api.getTriggerProps(), {\n    onPointerEnter: handleHover,\n  })\n\n  return (\n    // 4. spread the new props\n    \u003ca href=\"https://twitter.com/zag_js\" target=\"_blank\" {...triggerProps}\u003e\n      {api.open ? \"Open\" : \"Close\"}\n    \u003c/a\u003e\n  )\n}\n```\n\n## Id composition\n\nZag depends heavily on pure DOM queries to identify elements. This means every\nelement part needs to have a unique id.\n\nEach time you initiate the machine with the `useMachine` hook, you'll need to\nensure that you provide a unique id.\n\nIn most cases, you can rely on the framework providing a unique id for each\nmachine.\n\n### React\n\n```jsx\nimport * as accordion from \"@zag-js/accordion\"\nimport { useMachine, normalizeProps } from \"@zag-js/framework\"\nimport { useId } from \"react\"\n\nfunction Component() {\n  const service = useMachine(accordion.machine, { id: useId() })\n  const api = machine.connect(service, normalizeProps)\n\n  // ...\n}\n```\n\nSee [useId](https://react.dev/reference/react/useId).\n\n### Solid\n\n```jsx\nimport * as accordion from \"@zag-js/accordion\"\nimport { useMachine, normalizeProps } from \"@zag-js/solid\"\nimport { createUniqueId } from \"solid-js\"\n\nfunction Component() {\n  const service = useMachine(accordion.machine, { id: createUniqueId() })\n  const api = machine.connect(service, normalizeProps)\n\n  // ...\n}\n```\n\nSee\n[createUniqueId](https://docs.solidjs.com/reference/component-apis/create-unique-id).\n\n### Vue\n\n```html\n\u003cscript setup\u003e\n  import * as accordion from \"@zag-js/accordion\"\n  import { useMachine, normalizeProps } from \"@zag-js/vue\"\n  import { useId } from \"vue\"\n\n  const service = useMachine(accordion.machine, { id: useId() })\n  const api = machine.connect(service, normalizeProps)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003c!-- ... --\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n```\n\nSee [useId](https://vuejs.org/api/composition-api-helpers#useid).\n\n### Svelte\n\n```html\n\u003cscript\u003e\n  import * as accordion from \"@zag-js/accordion\"\n  import { useMachine, normalizeProps } from \"@zag-js/svelte\"\n\n  const id = $props.id()\n  const service = useMachine(accordion.machine, { id })\n  const api = machine.connect(service, normalizeProps)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003c!-- ... --\u003e\n```\n\nSee [$props.id](\u003chttps://svelte.dev/docs/svelte/$props#$props.id()\u003e).\n\nInternally, Zag maps the unique id provided to each component parts needed for\nthe widget to work.\n\nIn some cases, you might want to compose different machines together in a single\ncomponent. For example, you want to use the same trigger as a popover and\ntooltip trigger at the same time.\n\nTo achieve this, you will need to pass custom `ids` to the machine's context.\nThis will ensure that calling `document.getElementById(...)` within the tooltip\nand/or popover will return the same element.\n\n```tsx {6,10}\nimport * as tooltip from \"@zag-js/tooltip\"\nimport * as popover from \"@zag-js/popover\"\n\nfunction Example() {\n  const tooltipService = useMachine(tooltip.machine, {\n    ids: { trigger: \"id-1\" },\n  })\n\n  const popoverService = useMachine(popover.machine, {\n    ids: { trigger: \"id-1\" },\n  })\n\n  // ...\n}\n```\n\nIn the example above, you will notice that the popover and tooltip trigger share\nthe same id. That's how to compose machines together.\n\n### Important: Customizing IDs and ARIA attributes\n\n#### Always use the `ids` context option\n\nWhen customizing element IDs, always use the `ids` option in the machine context.\nNever manually set the `id` attribute on elements using the prop functions.\n\n```tsx\n// ❌ Wrong: Manually setting id on the element\nconst api = checkbox.connect(service, normalizeProps)\nreturn \u003clabel {...api.getLabelProps()} id=\"my-custom-id\"\u003eLabel\u003c/label\u003e\n\n// ✓ Correct: Use the ids option in machine context\nconst service = useMachine(checkbox.machine, {\n  ids: { label: \"my-custom-id\" },\n})\nconst api = checkbox.connect(service, normalizeProps)\nreturn \u003clabel {...api.getLabelProps()}\u003eLabel\u003c/label\u003e\n```\n\n**Why?** Zag needs to know about custom IDs to properly generate ARIA reference\nattributes across all related elements. When you set IDs manually, the machine\ncan't update the corresponding `aria-labelledby`, `aria-describedby`, and other\nreference attributes.\n\n#### Pitfall: Custom IDs with missing elements\n\nWhen you configure custom IDs via the `ids` option, Zag generates ARIA reference\nattributes (like `aria-labelledby`) based on those IDs, regardless of whether\nthe elements exist in the DOM. This can break accessibility if you configure IDs\nfor elements you don't render.\n\n```tsx\n// ❌ Wrong: Configuring label ID but not rendering the label\nconst service = useMachine(checkbox.machine, {\n  ids: { label: \"custom-label-id\" },\n})\nreturn (\n  \u003cdiv {...api.getControlProps()}\u003e\n    {/* Control has aria-labelledby=\"custom-label-id\" but label doesn't exist */}\n    \u003cinput {...api.getHiddenInputProps()} /\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n)\n\n// ✓ Correct: Only configure IDs for elements you render\nconst service = useMachine(checkbox.machine, {\n  ids: { control: \"custom-control-id\" },\n  // Don't set label ID if you're not rendering it\n})\nreturn (\n  \u003cdiv {...api.getControlProps()} aria-label=\"Checkbox\"\u003e\n    \u003cinput {...api.getHiddenInputProps()} /\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n)\n\n// ✓ Better: Keep the label but hide it visually\nreturn (\n  \u003cdiv\u003e\n    \u003clabel {...api.getLabelProps()} className=\"visually-hidden\"\u003e\n      Checkbox\n    \u003c/label\u003e\n    \u003cdiv {...api.getControlProps()}\u003e\n      \u003cinput {...api.getHiddenInputProps()} /\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n)\n```\n\n## Custom window environment\n\nInternally, we use DOM query methods like `document.querySelectorAll` and\n`document.getElementById` to locate elements within the machine.\n\nIn custom environments like iframe, Shadow DOM, Electron, etc., the machine\nmight not work as expected because `document` may not be available.\n\nTo provide the correct reference to root node or document, you can pass\n`getRootNode` function it to the machine's context.\n\n\u003e In shadow DOM, the root node can be derived from calling\n\u003e `element.getRootNode()` method on any element.\n\n```jsx {12,16,42}\nimport * as accordion from \"@zag-js/accordion\"\nimport { useMachine, normalizeProps } from \"@zag-js/react\"\nimport Frame, { useFrame } from \"react-frame-component\"\n\nconst data = [\n  { title: \"Watercraft\", content: \"Sample accordion content\" },\n  { title: \"Automobiles\", content: \"Sample accordion content\" },\n  { title: \"Aircraft\", content: \"Sample accordion content\" },\n]\n\nfunction Accordion({ id }) {\n  const { document } = useFrame()\n\n  const service = useMachine(accordion.machine, {\n    id,\n    getRootNode: () =\u003e document,\n  })\n\n  const api = accordion.connect(service, normalizeProps)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv {...api.getRootProps()}\u003e\n      {data.map((item, index) =\u003e (\n        \u003cdiv key={index} {...api.getItemProps({ value: item.title })}\u003e\n          \u003ch3\u003e\n            \u003cbutton {...api.getTriggerProps({ value: item.title })}\u003e\n              {item.title}\n            \u003c/button\u003e\n          \u003c/h3\u003e\n          \u003cdiv {...api.getContentProps({ value: item.title })}\u003e\n            {item.content}\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      ))}\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nexport default function App() {\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"App\"\u003e\n      \u003ch1\u003eZagJs in Iframe\u003c/h1\u003e\n      \u003cFrame height=\"200px\" width=\"100%\"\u003e\n        \u003cAccordion id=\"2\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Frame\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n```"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Composition\",\"description\":\"Best practices to compose events and
